< review>
This review has to broken into two parts, which combine for the score. The original work was to run electricity to our back yard for both a future spa (220) and a branch for a future BBQ installation (110). Initial work was completed with the understanding that the stub for the 110 was ready for when the BBQ was built (and would be tapped from) and that the 220 was ready for spa installation (spa-ready was the request). This work was done timely and the team was very nice and helpful.

Part 2 was when spa arrived, and what transpired since then. The 220 box did not have some necessary parts, and the offered help to explain what additional parts would be needed (as well as where to plug them in) in lieu of an additional $300 has not transpired. Pictures of the installation, the parts (wires and GFCI) as well as the spa manual have been provided and for two weeks I have gotten "we'll get back to you". I had held off approaching other options, but after 2 weeks I would really like to get my spa up and running and can't wait for answer any longer.

It is frustrating because spa-ready meant one thing to me and clearly something different to the installers. What was done was not ready for immediate installation (more than just the wire run was required) and the lack of response has not made me a long time fan.

I would recommend to anyone using their services to, as you would with any contractor, ensure that the results truly match your needs before you sign off. My fault for not fully understanding what I would need for the future spa setup, but I was relying on the professionals here and I paid for it (literally).<//review>

<date>1399598238016</date><pics>None<//pics><Rate>2</Rate>< text>
My husband and I decided to eat here after a few nights in San Francisco to have some seafood. We read the reviews and were convinced that it would be good. My husband had a salmon and shrimp scampi dish with a dinner salad and I had the scallops with a dinner salad. The dinner salads were about $10 for a plate full of iceberg lettuce and our main dishes left much to be desired for what we paid. We think that we could have gotten better quality and quantity seafood at Red Lobster for less. I suggest you go down the Marina to Joe's Crab Shack and get better food and pay less. The restaurant itself was old and dated. The restrooms were disgusting. Had I used it before dinner, we probably wouldn't have stayed.< /text>

<Rating>4</Rating><text>If you go to Sinbad's, prepare to step into a time machine that takes you back to the 70s and 80s.    The ceiling is dark cork, the checks are all hand-written, the lightbulbs are all incandescent and even the music was retro.  Seriously, they were playing the Carpenters and the BeeGees the whole evening we were there.  The debate after dinner was about whether the dated-ness is accidental or an intentional theme.   But if you're o.k. with that, you're in for a good dining experience.  The view was great, and the food was well-executed and very high quality, though hardly innovative.  For example, the dessert menu features chocolate cake, vanilla ice cream and for the most exotic offering, Cherries Jubilee.  But the ice cream, cake, and Jubilee were all delicious. The service was good, too.  The whole staff were an experienced bunch who were a well-oiled machine.  The prices were high, but understandably so, considering the location.< /text><Pictures>None<//Pictures>< Resp>

<rate>5< /rate>< Text>
Very helpful, knowledgeable, courteous.   Nice guy named Joe helped me  first on the phone,  then a while later, when I was able to get to the store.
One morning my battery was dead, not even a click from the starter, which I thought was unusual.   I called Auto Zone, and got info from Joe about my battery's warranty, about replacement, and so on.  He said he would run a diagnostic check on the battery and charging system.

After a long wait for help to arrive, I got the dead battery jump started. Then I drove around for a while, before I went to Auto Zone.  I shut off the car and immediately restarted it.  Seemed fine now.  I told Joe about the situation, that I thought the battery was actually fine.  Nonetheless Joe went out to my car and connected his meter to the battery, and got readings for the battery, the alternator and the voltage regulator.
Yes,  my battery and the charging system are fine.

It was a pleasure, and I was fortunate, to have Joe attending to my business with Auto Zone in Ramona.<//Text>

< text>
If you looking for a quiet out of the way place for excellent coffee and a to die for danish (blueberry), look no further. I've been working in that little nook area by the theater for years and it had been (how did that "critic" put it)...meh for a few years. A few shops had recently closed. These guys move in and it has really brought a lot of ambiance to the area. It's right around the fountain. One of the owners saw me working. He came out and just started chopping it up with me. Just a genuinely nice guy. He offered to make me a coffee. Let me say I am a dark roast, french roast, kind of guy. I usually take a pass when someone offers me a coffee. something, something, something...I take him up on on his offer and I was blown away. One of the best tasting cups, all the way to the last drop, I've had in awhile. I am going back for more. Everyone there treated me with a smile and kindness. Do yourself a favor...go there try one of the coffee's and just relax. Sit by the fountain and take a load off. There's not many places like this.</text>

<Name>Stefano Braca< /Name>< Text>
The Secret of this tiny little Restaurant is hidden beyond what's available on the menu...

IF THERE WAS A 7 STARS RATING, THIS PLACE DESERVES IT

This is not your conventional pure commercial Sushi Bar... the owner is right there, behind the counter, and talks to you, he asks you what are the flavors you like, and if you let him do his Magic...

WOW... i mean WOWOWOW!!!

What this guy can come up with in a matter of minutes for you it is incredible... the Menu is just to satisfy the common Sushi eaters that go around, but if you ask him to make you something Special off the menu, it will blow you away.

My only Regret:

i live in North Carolina, and i happen to travel for work every once in a while to California... since i discovered this place, any time i visit a Customer in the area, this is a MUST Stop.

I highly recommend this place to all my Friends that travel in that area, so far, everybody has been really happy

This place totally changed my scale of Good in Sushi, because this guy really well far off scale
